This update to Deeplearning.University has 362 new Deep Learning papers (all from 2015) collected in the period since last update (January 27th, 2015) and until today.  See the 362 new papers below, and <a href="http://deeplearning.university">deeplearning.university</a> for the entire updated bibliography (it has more than 1000 papers now, 1324 to be accurate).


<span style="color: #0000ff;"><em>As always if you want have suggestions to the bibliography (in particular: improved Bibtex-entries or additions), please do that as git pull-requests on the file: <a href="https://github.com/memkite/DeepLearningBibliography/blob/master/bibtex/deeplearninggpuwithkeywords2014.bib">https://github.com/memkite/DeepLearningBibliography/blob/master/bibtex/deeplearninggpuwithkeywords2014.bib</a></em></span>


Best regards,


<a href="http://memkite.com/team/">Amund Tveit </a>
